#STOPNAMES: 
# for person/org/all
# These names could not be part of a person/org name.
# If the grammar outputs a name containing such STOPNAME, 
#the name will be deleted.

# prefixes
al | GTYPE>name_prefix 
#al'| GTYPE>name_prefix | STRICT > (?i:al['´’‘`])
# abu = father of, umm = mother of 
abu | GTYPE>name_prefix
umm | GTYPE>name_prefix


# arabic infixes (can be prefixed as well)
# ibn = son of, bint = daughter of 
bin  | GTYPE>name_infix
bint | GTYPE>name_infix

de | GTYPE>name_infix
de la | GTYPE>name_infix
de los | GTYPE>name_infix
#del | GTYPE>name_infix #to ambiguous and does not hram removing it
#dal | GTYPE>name_infix #to ambiguous and does not hram removing it
de | GTYPE>name_infix
da | GTYPE>name_infix
v d | GTYPE>name_infix
#v | GTYPE>name_infix
van de | GTYPE>name_infix
van den | GTYPE>name_infix
van der | GTYPE>name_infix
van | GTYPE>name_infix
der | GTYPE>name_infix
von d | GTYPE>name_infix
von de | GTYPE>name_infix
von den | GTYPE>name_infix
von der | GTYPE>name_infix	
von | GTYPE>name_infix

# suffixes

IV. |GTYPE> name_suffix  | STRICT > (?i:IV\.?)
